<div id="review_1968193893" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1968193893" />
    <a title="booksnpenguins" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/66222749-booksnpenguins"><img alt="booksnpenguins" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580407796p2/66222749.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1968193893?book_show_action=true">Jan 10, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="booksnpenguins" class="user" itemprop="url" name="booksnpenguins" href="/user/show/66222749-booksnpenguins">booksnpenguins</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/29486766-strange-the-dreamer">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">All the dreamers </span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to booksnpenguins by: </span>
      Marceline 
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66222749-booksnpenguins?shelf=shippity-ship-ship">shippity-ship-ship</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66222749-booksnpenguins?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1968193893" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15620146499799708839"><blockquote>
  <i>As a boy at the abbey, stories had been Lazlo's only wealth. <br/>He was richer now.<br/>Now he had books.</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><br/>Those of you who’ve been following my reviews and rant-views for a while, already know that my first experience with Laini Taylor and her Daughter of.. was a complete failure.<br/>I kind of enjoyed the writing, even if I found it a little pompous and confusing, and the plot was not bad either, but my main problems were the characters and their interactions. <br/>I couldn’t be happier to admit that Strange t</span>
  <span id="freeText15620146499799708839" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>As a boy at the abbey, stories had been Lazlo's only wealth. <br>He was richer now.<br>Now he had books.</i>
</blockquote><br><br><br>Those of you who’ve been following my reviews and rant-views for a while, already know that my first experience with Laini Taylor and her Daughter of.. was a complete failure.<br>I kind of enjoyed the writing, even if I found it a little pompous and confusing, and the plot was not bad either, but my main problems were the characters and their interactions. <br>I couldn’t be happier to admit that Strange the Dreamer made me change my mind and it did it in a way such that I’ll probably never stop thinking about this book. <br>I loved everything about this book.<br><a href="https://gifyu.com/image/LKNj" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1516374050ra/24892438.gif" alt="giphy3484a06d908f530f.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>The characters are all so amazing and well-crafted, even the evil ones.<br>Lazlo is simply adorable and incredibly relatable. I think his passion for everything bookish is admirable and something that we all can identify with, especially us Goodreads people. <br>I felt a deep connection with both him and Sarai, and their love is so pure and sweet that it makes you want to find your soulmate and fall in love for the rest of your life. <br><blockquote>
  <i>"Do you still think I'm a...a singularly unhorrible demon?"<br>"No," he said, smiling. "I think you're a fairy tale. I think you're magical, and brave and exquisite. And..." His voice grew bashful. Only in a dream could he be so bold and speak such words. "I hope you'll let me be in your story."</i>
</blockquote><br>I also particularly liked Sparrow and Ruby’s sisterly relationship, Calixte's witty bits, Shueyla's spirit and Eril-Fane and Azareen's mutual grief.<br><br>The setting is fantastic, it helps with the pace of the story and it creates the right dream-like atmosphere. <br>I think the problem with Laini Taylor and urban/modern settings, is that her imagination is so wild and big that, when it has to be contained or confined into a space and a story that follow determined rules, it loses half of its perfection.<br>So, yeah, the fact that Strange the Dreamer takes place in a world that the author’s created from the ground up, does nothing but add positive points to the final outcome.<br>Again, what I enjoyed the most was the writing. <br>Nothing beats the writing.<br>The author has a way with words that leaves you stunned, incredulously wondering how can someone even think of putting those simple words together and form coherent, unforgettable and striking lines like those ones.<br>Said this, I can’t help but mention all those wonderful quotes *_________* they’ll definitely stay with me forever. <br><blockquote>
  <i>Its emptiness was stark. The room felt hollow and dead, like a body with its hearts cut out. Breathing wasn't easy. <br>He dropped onto the edge of his bed.<br>"They're only books," he told himself. Just paper and ink.<br>Paper, ink, and years. <br>Paper, ink, years, and dreams.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>I adore Strange the Dreamer, it's the perfect story for those who aren't afraid to dream. <br>It also doesn't hurt that it was recommended to me by someone I admire and love very much. It makes this book twice as special. <br><br>The twists tho... <br><b>WHAT</b><br><a href="http://it.tinypic.com?ref=s16oa8" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1516378023ra/24892523.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>THE</b><br><a href="http://it.tinypic.com?ref=243jl6v" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1516378023ra/24892522.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>FECK</b><br><a href="http://it.tinypic.com?ref=161j70o" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1516378023ra/24892524.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1585673329i/29206385.png" width="80" height="80" alt="Professional Reader" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1585673329i/29206386.png" width="80" height="80" alt="10 Book Reviews" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1585673329i/29206384.png" width="80" height="80" alt="Reviews Published" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('GeiF5o3uLYu9qC1xrf84GuF8fbilPk2AVTOxpnwfVCNw2h1C61DPHnH5BdXjG4RVyWEnwR2ykTyA/6Pl9xOGUA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('kxJozkjjVZVOrRW5iplhA8E1nLZ4uoVcNRYQepCPYvz6IPBqLl23AIL8PR3Efd1M6SjGz8A2WeDg2gI5G4Owjw==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer11876349531501462753">Hi! I write fantasy books. My latest is STRANGE THE DREAMER, about a young librarian, a mythic lost city, and the half-human children of murdered gods. Check it out :-) Before that I wrote the DAUGHTER OF SMOKE & BONE trilogy, which has been translated into 32 languages. It's about a blue-haired art student raised by monsters, a broken angel, and a war that has raged for 1000 years in another worl</span>
  <span id="freeText11876349531501462753" style="display:none">Hi! I write fantasy books. My latest is STRANGE THE DREAMER, about a young librarian, a mythic lost city, and the half-human children of murdered gods. Check it out :-) Before that I wrote the DAUGHTER OF SMOKE &amp; BONE trilogy, which has been translated into 32 languages. It's about a blue-haired art student raised by monsters, a broken angel, and a war that has raged for 1000 years in another world. I also wrote LIPS TOUCH: THREE TIMES, which was a National Book Award finalist, and the DREAMDARK books. As well as various short stories and novellas. <br /><br />Thanks for reading!! <br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.lainitaylor.com">www.lainitaylor.com</a><br /><br />@lainitaylor</span>

            if ($('bookCover_25446343').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('bookCover_25446343').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>
